	ModPlayVoiceLS(4, 9, "ps3/s13/09/550500223", 128, TRUE);
	OutputLine(NULL, "「くすくすくすあはははははは！",
		   NULL, "\"Eheheheh... ahahahahah!", Line_WaitForInput);
	ModPlayVoiceLS(4, 9, "ps3/s13/09/550500224", 128, TRUE);
	OutputLine(NULL, "　ならば結構、かかっておいでなさい！！",
		   NULL, " Bene, allora non perdiamo altro tempo!", Line_WaitForInput);
	ModPlayVoiceLS(4, 9, "ps3/s13/09/550500225", 128, TRUE);
	OutputLine(NULL, "　どちらの想いが強いか！",
		   NULL, " Scopriremo presto chi possiede il volere più forte!", Line_WaitForInput);
	ModPlayVoiceLS(4, 9, "ps3/s13/09/550500226", 128, TRUE);
	OutputLine(NULL, "　強かった方が未来を作る。",
		   NULL, " Sarà il vincitore di questo confronto a plasmare il futuro.", Line_WaitForInput);
	ModPlayVoiceLS(4, 9, "ps3/s13/09/550500227", 128, TRUE);
	OutputLine(NULL, "強かった方の望んだ未来が訪れる。",
		   NULL, " Il futuro scelto da chi ha avuto la forza di compierlo.", GetGlobalFlag(GLinemodeSp));
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLine("<color=#f6d9a8>鷹野</color>", NULL, "<color=#f6d9a8>Takano</color>", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	ModPlayVoiceLS(4, 9, "ps3/s13/09/550500228", 128, TRUE);
	OutputLine(NULL, "私は私の未来を一歩も譲らない！",
		   NULL, "Sappi che non indietreggerò neppure di un passo!", Line_WaitForInput);
	ModPlayVoiceLS(4, 9, "ps3/s13/09/550500229", 128, TRUE);
	OutputLine(NULL, "　その未来では祖父の偉業は讃えられ神となり、かつて私を不幸にて試すような真似をした神に対して復讐をする。」",
		   NULL, " Nel mio futuro, il lavoro di mio nonno verrà acclamato e lo trasformerà in un dio! E io avrò la mia rivincita contro colui che mi ha posto solo dinnanzi a sfide e dolori!\"", Line_Normal);
	ClearMessage();

	DrawScene( "black", 1000 );

	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLineAll("", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	OutputLine(NULL, "　くすくすくす、あっはははははははっはっはっは！！",
		   NULL, "Eheheheh, ahahahah! AhahahAHAHAHAH!!", Line_WaitForInput);
	OutputLine(NULL, "　間抜けなチビ神め！",
		   NULL, " Piccola e patetica dea!", Line_WaitForInput);
	OutputLine(NULL, "　身の程を思い知らせてやる！",
		   NULL, " Te la farò vedere io!", Line_Normal);
	ClearMessage();

	ModSetLayerFilter(2, 256, "none");
	ModDrawCharacter(2, 9, "sprite/ta1_iradachi_", "0", 0, 0, 0, FALSE, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 10, 0, FALSE );
	DrawScene( "background/ji2", 1000 );
	FadeBustshot( 2, FALSE, 0, 0, 0, 0, 200, TRUE );
	StartShakingOfWindow( 248, 30, 0, 2, 2*2, FALSE );
	StartShakingOfAllObjects( 248, 30, 0, 2, 2*2, FALSE );
	ModSetLayerFilter(1, 256, "none");
	ModDrawCharacter(1, 9, "portrait/ta1_iradachi_", "0", 0, 0, 0, FALSE, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 100, TRUE );

	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLine("<color=#f6d9a8>鷹野</color>", NULL, "<color=#f6d9a8>Takano</color>", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	ModPlayVoiceLS(4, 9, "ps3/s13/09/550500230", 128, TRUE);
	OutputLine(NULL, "「貴様を神の座から引き摺り下ろしてやる！！",
		   NULL, "\"Ti trascinerò giù con la forza dal tuo falso trono!!", GetGlobalFlag(GLinemodeSp));
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { ClearMessage(); } else { OutputLineAll(NULL, "\n", Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }

	DisableWindow();
	ModDrawCharacter(1, 9, "portrait/ta1_sakebi_", "2", 0, 0, 0, FALSE, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 200, TRUE );

	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLine("<color=#f6d9a8>鷹野</color>", NULL, "<color=#f6d9a8>Takano</color>", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	ModPlayVoiceLS(4, 9, "ps3/s13/09/550500231", 128, TRUE);
	OutputLine(NULL, "　かかってこい、この――――！！」",
		   NULL, "Fatti sotto!!!\"", Line_Normal);
	ClearMessage();

	CallScript( "&eye" );
	SetValidityOfInput( FALSE );
	Wait( 1000 );
	SetValidityOfInput( TRUE );
	DrawScene( "prologue/matu_t1", 5000 );
	SetValidityOfInput( FALSE );
	Wait( 7000 );
	SetValidityOfInput( TRUE );
	DrawScene( "prologue/matu_t2", 1000 );
	SetValidityOfInput( FALSE );
	Wait( 7000 );
	SetValidityOfInput( TRUE );

	DrawScene( "black", 3000 );
	FadeOutBGM( 0, 1000, TRUE );
	SetSpeedOfMessage( FALSE, 0 );
	ModCallScriptSection("&opening", "OpeningStory");
}
